Here's what's going on:

1. **개** means "me" or "my" in Korean.
2. **인** is a verb, which means "to gamble" or "to play games".
3. **재** is a noun, which means "assets" or "wealth".
4. **를** is a particle to indicate the action of the previous word.

So, the phrase "개인 전 재" can be translated as "Me (I) have (got) assets".
